class="post-2106 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-malwareanalysis ast-article-single" id="post-2106" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork" itemscope="itemscope">

	
	
<div class="ast-post-format- ast-no-thumb single-layout-1">

	
	
		<header class="entry-header ast-no-thumbnail">

			
			<h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">A detailed analysis of the STOP/Djvu Ransomware</h1><div class="entry-meta">By <span class="posted-by vcard author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="author">			<a title="View all posts by CyberMasterV"
				href="https://cybergeeks.tech/author/cybermaster/" rel="author"
				class="url fn n" itemprop="url"				>
				<span
				class="author-name" itemprop="name"				>
				CyberMasterV			</span>
			</a>
		</span>

		 / <span class="posted-on"><span class="published" itemprop="datePublished"> October 31, 2021 </span></span> / <span class="ast-terms-link"><a href="https://cybergeeks.tech/category/malwareanalysis/" class="">Malware analysis</a></span></div>
			
		</header><!-- .entry-header -->

	
	
	<div class="entry-content clear"
	itemprop="text"	>

		
		
<p style="font-size:25px">Summary </p>



<p>STOP/Djvu ransomware is not a very known ransomware like Conti, REvil or BlackMatter, however ESET ranked it on the 3rd place in the top ransomware families in Q2 2020 (<a href="https://www.welivesecurity.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESET_Threat_Report_Q22020.pdf">https://www.welivesecurity.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESET_Threat_Report_Q22020.pdf</a>). This ransomware can run with one of the following parameters: “–Admin”, “–Task”, “–AutoStart”, “–ForNetRes”, and “–Service”. The process doesn&#8217;t target specific countries based on their country code, and also decrypts a list of files, file extensions and folders that will be skipped. Two persistence mechanisms are implemented: a Run registry key and a scheduled task created using COM objects. The malware computes the MD5 hash of the MAC address and performs a GET request to the C2 server based on it. The binary also acts as a downloader for 2 malicious files called build2.exe and build3.exe. The victim ID is decrypted using the XOR operator and then written to a file called PersonalID.txt. Both local drives and network shares are targeted by the malware, and the files are encrypted using the Salsa20 algorithm. The Salsa20 matrix used for encrypting files is based on a UUID generated using the UuidCreate API, which is encrypted using an embedded RSA public key (if the C2 server is unreachable) or a public key downloaded from the C2 server. The RSA implementation found in the executable is taken from the OpenSSL project hosted at <a href="https://github.com/openssl/openssl">https://github.com/openssl/openssl</a>.</p>



<p><strong>Analyst</strong>: <a href="https://twitter.com/GeeksCyber">@GeeksCyber</a></p>



<p style="font-size:25px">Technical analysis </p>



<p>SHA256: 4380c45fd46d1a63cffe4d37cf33b0710330a766b7700af86020a936cdd09cbe</p>



<p>The following PDB path can be found in the binary: &#8220;C:\xudihiguhe\jegovicatusoca\jijetogez\winucet\xusev\kucor.pdb&#8221;. There is a call to GlobalAlloc that allocates several bytes from the heap:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="1024" height="113" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/1-1024x113.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2113" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/1-1024x113.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/1-300x33.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/1-768x85.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/1.jpg 1178w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 1</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malware calls the LoadLibraryW function in order to load the &#8220;kernel32.dll&#8221; file into the address space of the process:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="1024" height="96" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/2-1024x96.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2116" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/2-1024x96.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/2-300x28.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/2-768x72.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/2.jpg 1179w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 2</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The GetProcAddress API is utilized to retrieve the address of the &#8220;VirtualProtect&#8221; function:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="1178" height="142" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/3-1024x123.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2117" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/3-1024x123.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/3-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/3-768x93.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/3.jpg 1178w" sizes="(max-width: 1178px) 100vw, 1178px" /><figcaption>Figure 3</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The memory area allocated above is filled in by the malware, and the VirtualProtect routine is used to change its protection to 0x40 = <strong>PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE</strong>:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="186" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/4-1024x186.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2118" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/4-1024x186.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/4-300x54.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/4-768x140.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/4.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 4</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>There is also a lot of garbage code in the binary that is never executed, as shown in figure 5:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="654" height="666" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/5-1.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2120" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/5-1.jpg 654w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/5-1-295x300.jpg 295w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 654px) 100vw, 654px" /><figcaption>Figure 5</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The process jumps at the beginning of the new shellcode, as highlighted below:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="821" height="356" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/6.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2122" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/6.jpg 821w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/6-300x130.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/6-768x333.jpg 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 821px) 100vw, 821px" /><figcaption>Figure 6</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The binary retrieves the address of the following functions using GetProcAddress: &#8220;GlobalAlloc&#8221;, &#8220;GetLastError&#8221;, &#8220;Sleep&#8221;, &#8220;VirtualAlloc&#8221;, &#8220;CreateToolhelp32Snapshot&#8221;, &#8220;Module32First&#8221;, &#8220;CloseHandle&#8221;. CreateToolhelp32Snapshot&nbsp;is utilized to take a snapshot of the current process that includes all its modules (0x8 = <strong>TH32CS_SNAPMODULE</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="113" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/7-1024x113.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2124" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/7-1024x113.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/7-300x33.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/7-768x85.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/7.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 7</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ransomware extracts information about the first module of the process using the Module32First&nbsp;API:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="114" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/8-1024x114.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2125" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/8-1024x114.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/8-300x33.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/8-768x85.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/8.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 8</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malicious process allocates and populates a new memory area via a function call to VirtualAlloc (0x1000 = <strong>MEM_COMMIT</strong> and 0x40 = <strong>PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="178" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/9-1024x178.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2126" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/9-1024x178.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/9-300x52.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/9-768x134.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/9.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 9</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The process jumps at the beginning of the new shellcode, as highlighted below:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="818" height="355" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/10.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2127" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/10.jpg 818w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/10-300x130.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/10-768x333.jpg 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 818px) 100vw, 818px" /><figcaption>Figure 10</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malware calls the LoadLibraryA API to load the following DLLs into memory: user32.dll, kernel32.dll and ntdll.dll. It also retrieves the address of the following functions: &#8220;MessageBoxA&#8221;, &#8220;GetMessageExtraInfo&#8221;, &#8220;WinExec&#8221;, &#8220;CreateFileA&#8221;, &#8220;WriteFile&#8221;, &#8220;CloseHandle&#8221;, &#8220;CreateProcessA&#8221;, &#8220;GetThreadContext&#8221;, &#8220;VirtualAlloc&#8221;, &#8220;VirtualAllocEx&#8221;, &#8220;VirtualFree&#8221;, &#8220;ReadProcessMemory&#8221;, &#8220;WriteProcessMemory&#8221;, &#8220;SetThreadContext&#8221;, &#8220;ResumeThread&#8221;, &#8220;WaitForSingleObject&#8221;, &#8220;GetModuleFileNameA&#8221;, &#8220;GetCommandLineA&#8221;, &#8220;NtUnmapViewOfSection&#8221;, &#8220;NtWriteVirtualMemory&#8221;, &#8220;RegisterClassExA&#8221;, &#8220;CreateWindowExA&#8221;, &#8220;PostMessageA&#8221;, &#8220;GetMessageA&#8221;, &#8220;DefWindowProcA&#8221;, &#8220;GetFileAttributesA&#8221;, &#8220;GetStartupInfoA&#8221;, &#8220;VirtualProtectEx&#8221;, &#8220;ExitProcess&#8221;.</p>



<p>From our perspective, the malware developers have implemented some actions that don&#8217;t influence the main execution flow as an anti-analysis mechanism. GetFileAttributesA&nbsp;is used to retrieve file system attributes for a non-existent file:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="115" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/11-1024x115.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2130" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/11-1024x115.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/11-300x34.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/11-768x86.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/11.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 11</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The file registers a window class called &#8220;saodkfnosa9uin&#8221; using the RegisterClassExA routine:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="166" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/12-1024x166.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2131" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/12-1024x166.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/12-300x49.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/12-768x125.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/12.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 12</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The CreateWindowExA&nbsp;function is utilized to create a new window (0x200 = <strong>WS_EX_CLIENTEDGE</strong>, 0xCF0000 = <strong>WS_OVERLAPPEDWINDOW</strong>, 0x80000000 = <strong>CW_USEDEFAULT</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="341" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/13-1024x341.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2132" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/13-1024x341.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/13-300x100.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/13-768x256.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/13.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 13</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The process allocates a new memory area via a function call to VirtualAlloc (0x1000 = <strong>MEM_COMMIT</strong> and 0x4 = <strong>PAGE_READWRITE</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="170" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/14-1024x170.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2133" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/14-1024x170.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/14-300x50.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/14-768x128.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/14.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 14</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ransomware extracts the content of the STARTUPINFO structure:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="113" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/15-1024x113.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2135" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/15-1024x113.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/15-300x33.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/15-768x85.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/15.jpg 1179w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 15</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malware creates a copy of itself in a suspended state via a call to CreateProcessA (0x08000004 = <strong>CREATE_NO_WINDOW</strong> | <strong>CREATE_SUSPENDED</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="332" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/16-1024x332.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2137" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/16-1024x332.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/16-300x97.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/16-768x249.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/16.jpg 1177w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 16</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>GetThreadContext&nbsp;is used to retrieve the context of a specific thread:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="142" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/17-1024x142.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2138" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/17-1024x142.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/17-300x42.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/17-768x106.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/17.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 17</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malicious binary unmaps a view of a section from the address of the newly created process using ZwUnmapViewOfSection:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="142" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/18-1024x142.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2139" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/18-1024x142.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/18-300x42.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/18-768x106.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/18.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 18</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The VirtualAllocEx&nbsp;routine is utilized to allocate new space in the newly created process (0x3000 = <strong>MEM_COMMIT</strong> | <strong>MEM_RESERVE</strong> and 0x40 = <strong>PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="236" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/19-1024x236.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2140" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/19-1024x236.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/19-300x69.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/19-768x177.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/19.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 19</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ransomware writes data to the area allocated above using multiple calls to ZwWriteVirtualMemory, as displayed in figure 20:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="956" height="1024" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/20-956x1024.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2141" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/20-956x1024.jpg 956w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/20-280x300.jpg 280w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/20-768x823.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/20.jpg 1180w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 956px) 100vw, 956px" /><figcaption>Figure 20</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The SetThreadContext&nbsp;function is used to set the context for the remote thread:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="142" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/21-1024x142.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2143" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/21-1024x142.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/21-300x42.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/21-768x106.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/21.jpg 1178w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 21</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The binary resumes the main thread of the suspended process using ResumeThread:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="113" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/22-1024x113.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2144" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/22-1024x113.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/22-300x33.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/22-768x85.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/22.jpg 1179w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 22</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>We&#8217;ve extracted the executable from memory, and we continue to analyze this file. The following PDB path has been found: &#8220;e:\doc\my work (c++)_git\encryption\release\encrypt_win_api.pdb&#8221;. The binary initializes the use of the WinINet functions by calling the InternetOpenW API (the user agent being &#8220;Microsoft Internet Explorer&#8221;):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="168" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/23-1024x168.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2147" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/23-1024x168.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/23-300x49.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/23-768x126.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/23.jpg 1167w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 23</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malware performs a GET request to https[:]//api.2ip.ua/geo.json, which reveals details about the location of the IP address:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="226" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/24-1024x226.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2148" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/24-1024x226.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/24-300x66.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/24-768x169.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/24.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 24</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>InternetReadFile is used to read the response from the server, and an example of a JSON form is displayed below:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="387" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/25-1024x387.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2149" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/25-1024x387.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/25-300x113.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/25-768x290.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/25.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 25</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The &#8220;country_code&#8221; element is compared with &#8220;RU&#8221; (Russian language), &#8220;BY&#8221; (Belarusian language), &#8220;UA&#8221; (Ukrainian language), &#8220;AZ&#8221; (Azerbaijani language), &#8220;AM&#8221; (Armenian language), &#8220;TJ&#8221; (Tajik language), &#8220;KZ&#8221; (Kazakh language), &#8220;KG&#8221; (Kyrgyz language), &#8220;UZ&#8221; (Uzbek language) and &#8220;SY&#8221; (Syriac language):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="43" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/26-1024x43.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2150" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/26-1024x43.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/26-300x12.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/26-768x32.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/26.jpg 1179w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 26</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The systems that have one of the languages enumerated above will not be encrypted. The priority for the current process is set to high by calling the SetPriorityClass routine (0x80 = <strong>HIGH_PRIORITY_CLASS</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="112" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/27-1024x112.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2151" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/27-1024x112.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/27-300x33.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/27-768x84.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/27.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 27</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The executable retrieves the command-line string for the process and then returns an array of pointers to the command-line arguments:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="130" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/28-1024x130.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2152" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/28-1024x130.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/28-300x38.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/28-768x98.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/28.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 28</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>It&#8217;s important to mention that the malware can run with one of the following parameters: &#8220;&#8211;Admin&#8221;, &#8220;&#8211;Task&#8221;, &#8220;&#8211;AutoStart&#8221;, &#8220;&#8211;ForNetRes&#8221;, and &#8220;&#8211;Service&#8221;. We&#8217;ll describe the execution flows with different parameters later on.</p>



<p>All process IDs that correspond to the processes on the system are retrieved by calling the EnumProcesses API:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="144" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/29-1024x144.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2155" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/29-1024x144.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/29-300x42.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/29-768x108.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/29.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 29</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>Each process object is opened by the ransomware using OpenProcess (0x410 = <strong>PROCESS_QUERY_INFORMATION</strong> | <strong>PROCESS_VM_READ</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="133" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/30-1024x133.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2157" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/30-1024x133.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/30-300x39.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/30-768x100.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/30.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 30</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The malware extracts a handle for each module from a process that was successfully opened:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="160" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/31-1024x160.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2158" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/31-1024x160.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/31-300x47.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/31-768x120.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/31.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 31</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The GetModuleBaseNameW&nbsp;function is used to retrieve the base name of a module that is compared with the name of the executable (in our case, &#8220;wininet_dump.exe&#8221;):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="163" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/32-1024x163.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2159" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/32-1024x163.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/32-300x48.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/32-768x122.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/32.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 32</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The binary performs a lot of XOR operations (key = 0x80) in order to decrypt relevant strings. The next figure contains a buffer with the C2 server securebiz[.]org:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="522" height="299" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/33.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2162" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/33.jpg 522w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/33-300x172.jpg 300w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 522px) 100vw, 522px" /><figcaption>Figure 33</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ransomware opens the Run registry key using RegOpenKeyExW (0x80000001 = <strong>HKEY_CURRENT_USER&nbsp;</strong>and 0xF003F = <strong>KEY_ALL_ACCESS</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="223" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/34-1024x223.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2164" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/34-1024x223.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/34-300x65.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/34-768x167.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/34.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 34</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The process is looking for a value called &#8220;SysHelper&#8221;, which doesn&#8217;t exist at this time:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="208" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/35-1024x208.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2166" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/35-1024x208.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/35-300x61.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/35-768x156.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/35.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 35</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The UuidCreate&nbsp;function is used to generate a new UUID (16 random bytes):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="118" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/36-1024x118.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2169" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/36-1024x118.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/36-300x35.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/36-768x89.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/36.jpg 1171w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 36</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The process converts the UUID to a string using the UuidToStringW&nbsp;API:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="182" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/37-1024x182.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2170" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/37-1024x182.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/37-300x53.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/37-768x137.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/37.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 37</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>A new directory based on the UUID is created by the malware:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="212" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/38-1024x212.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2171" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/38-1024x212.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/38-300x62.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/38-768x159.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/38.jpg 1179w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 38</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The CopyFileW&nbsp;routine is utilized to copy the executable to a new file in the above directory:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="149" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/39-1024x149.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2172" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/39-1024x149.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/39-300x44.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/39-768x111.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/39.jpg 1179w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 39</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ransomware establishes persistence on the host by creating an entry called &#8220;SysHelper&#8221; under the Run registry key, which will run the executable with the &#8220;&#8211;AutoStart&#8221; parameter whenever the user logs on:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="289" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/40-1024x289.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2173" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/40-1024x289.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/40-300x85.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/40-768x217.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/40.jpg 1179w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 40</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The binary denies &#8220;Everyone&#8221; to delete the folder created above using the icacls command, as highlighted in figure 41:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="350" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/41-1024x350.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2174" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/41-1024x350.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/41-300x102.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/41-768x262.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/41.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 41</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>A second persistence mechanism consists of creating a scheduled task (using COM objects) that will run the ransomware every 5 minutes.</p>



<p>The malicious file initializes the COM library on the current thread using the CoInitialize function:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="103" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/42-1024x103.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2176" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/42-1024x103.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/42-300x30.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/42-768x77.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/42.jpg 1172w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 42</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>We have observed that the implementation is similar to the one presented at <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/win32/taskschd/time-trigger-example--c---">https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/win32/taskschd/time-trigger-example&#8211;c&#8212;</a>, however we&#8217;ll dig deeper and explain how the assembly code looks like. </p>



<p>The CoInitializeSecurity routine is used to register and set the default security values for the process (0x6 = <strong>RPC_C_AUTHN_LEVEL_PKT_PRIVACY</strong> and 0x3 = <strong>RPC_C_IMP_LEVEL_IMPERSONATE</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="248" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/43-1024x248.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2178" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/43-1024x248.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/43-300x73.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/43-768x186.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/43.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 43</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The process creates an object with the CLSID {0F87369F-A4E5-4CFC-BD3E-73E6154572DD}, which implements the Schedule.Service class for operating the Windows Task Scheduler Service:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="180" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/44-1024x180.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2179" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/44-1024x180.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/44-300x53.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/44-768x135.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/44.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 44</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>You can notice if you follow the C++ implementation mentioned above that in a case of a function call such as p -&gt; f(a,b), the assembly representation contains 3 parameters pushed on the stack (because the pointer p is pushed as well). An example of such a call is represented by the ITaskService::GetFolder method, which gets a folder of registered tasks:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="140" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/45-1024x140.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2180" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/45-1024x140.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/45-300x41.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/45-768x105.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/45.jpg 1171w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 45</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>A task called &#8220;Time Trigger Task&#8221; is deleted using the ITaskFolder::DeleteTask method:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="140" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/46-1024x140.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2181" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/46-1024x140.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/46-300x41.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/46-768x105.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/46.jpg 1167w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 46</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ITaskService::NewTask function is utilized to create an empty task definition object:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="152" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/47-1024x152.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2182" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/47-1024x152.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/47-300x44.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/47-768x114.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/47.jpg 1168w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 47</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>An example of a safe release when the pointer is no longer used is shown in figure 48:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="103" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/48-1024x103.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2183" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/48-1024x103.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/48-300x30.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/48-768x78.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/48.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 48</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The binary retrieves the registration information of the task (the description, the author, and the date the task is registered) by calling the ITaskDefinition::get_RegistrationInfo method:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="123" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/49-1024x123.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2184" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/49-1024x123.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/49-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/49-768x92.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/49.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 49</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>IRegistrationInfo::put_Author is used to set the author of the task to &#8220;Author Name&#8221;:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="121" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/50-1024x121.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2185" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/50-1024x121.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/50-300x35.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/50-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/50.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 50</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The ransomware retrieves the principal for the task (which provides the security credentials) by calling the ITaskDefinition::get_Principal function:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="122" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/51-1024x122.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2186" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/51-1024x122.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/51-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/51-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/51.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 51</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The security logon type is set to 0x3 (<strong>TASK_LOGON_INTERACTIVE_TOKEN</strong>), which means that the task will be run only in an existing interactive session:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="121" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/52-1024x121.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2187" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/52-1024x121.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/52-300x35.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/52-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/52.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 52</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>ITaskDefinition::get_Settings is utilized to retrieve the settings that describe how the Task Scheduler performs the task:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="122" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/53-1024x122.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2190" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/53-1024x122.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/53-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/53-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/53.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 53</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The file sets a Boolean value to 0xFFFFFFFF (<strong>VARIANT_TRUE</strong>) that indicates the Task Scheduler can start the task at any time after its scheduled time has elapsed using the ITaskSettings::put_StartWhenAvailable method:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="121" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/54-1024x121.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2191" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/54-1024x121.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/54-300x35.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/54-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/54.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 54</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The amount of time the Task Scheduler will wait for an idle condition to occur is set to 5 minutes via a function call to IIdleSettings::put_WaitTimeout:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="122" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/55-1024x122.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2193" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/55-1024x122.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/55-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/55-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/55.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 55</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>ITaskDefinition::get_Triggers is used to get a collection of triggers used to start the task:</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="122" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/56-1024x122.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2195" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/56-1024x122.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/56-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/56-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/56.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 56</figcaption></figure></div>



<p>The executable creates a new trigger for the task using the ITriggerCollection::Create method (0x1 = <strong>TASK_TRIGGER_TIME</strong>):</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="150" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/57-1024x150.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2196" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/57-1024x150.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/57-300x44.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/57-768x112.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/57.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 57</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="167" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/58-1024x167.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2197" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/58-1024x167.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/58-300x49.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/58-768x125.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/58.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 58</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="122" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/59-1024x122.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2198" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/59-1024x122.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/59-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/59-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/59.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 59</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="122" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/60-1024x122.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2199" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/60-1024x122.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/60-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/60-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/60.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 60</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="94" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/61-1024x94.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2200" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/61-1024x94.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/61-300x27.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/61-768x70.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/61.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 61</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="193" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/62-1024x193.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2201" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/62-1024x193.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/62-300x57.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/62-768x145.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/62.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 62</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="121" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/63-1024x121.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2202" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/63-1024x121.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/63-300x35.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/63-768x91.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/63.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 63</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="151" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/64-1024x151.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2203" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/64-1024x151.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/64-300x44.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/64-768x113.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/64.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 64</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1170" height="188" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/65-1024x165.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2205" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/65-1024x165.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/65-300x48.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/65-768x123.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/65.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1170px) 100vw, 1170px" /><figcaption>Figure 65</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="233" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/66-1024x233.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2207" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/66-1024x233.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/66-300x68.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/66-768x175.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/66.jpg 1169w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 66</figcaption></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="123" src="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/67-1024x123.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-2208" srcset="https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/67-1024x123.jpg 1024w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/67-300x36.jpg 300w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/67-768x93.jpg 768w, https://cybergeeks.tech/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/67.jpg 1170w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption>Figure 67</figcaption></figure></div>
